Research	O

(L2)	O

L2.	EOS

1.1	O
What	O
is	O
Government?	EOS
DIFFERENT	O
TYPES	O
OF	O
GOVERNMENT	EOS
The	O
government	O
of	O
the	O
United	O
States	O
can	O
best	O
be	O
described	O
as	O
a	O
republic,	O
or	O
representative	O
democracy.	EOS
A	O
democracy	O
is	O
a	O
government	O
in	O
which	O
political	O
power—influence	O
over	O
institutions,	O
leaders,	O
and	O
policies—rests	O
in	O
the	O
hands	O
of	O
the	O
people.	EOS
In	O
a	O
representative	O
democracy,	O
however,	O
the	O
citizens	O
do	O
not	O
govern	O
directly.	EOS
Instead,	O
they	O
elect	O
representatives	O
to	O
make	O
decisions	O
and	O
pass	O
laws	O
on	O
behalf	O
of	O
all	O
the	O
people.	EOS
Thus,	O
U.S.	O
citizens	O
vote	O
for	O
members	O
of	O
Congress,	O
the	O
president	O
and	O
vice	O
president,	O
members	O
of	O
state	O
legislatures,	O
governors,	O
mayors,	O
and	O
members	O
of	O
town	O
councils	O
and	O
school	O
boards	O
to	O
act	O
on	O
their	O
behalf.	EOS

Most	O
representative	O
governments	O
favor	O
majority	O
rule:	EOS
the	O
opinions	O
of	O
the	O
majority	O
of	O
the	O
people	O
have	O
more	O
influence	O
with	O
government	O
than	O
those	O
of	O
the	O
minority.	EOS
If	O
the	O
number	O
of	O
elected	O
representatives	O
who	O
favor	O
a	O
proposed	O
law	O
is	O
greater	O
than	O
those	O
who	O
oppose	O
it,	O
the	O
law	O
will	O
be	O
enacted.	EOS
However,	O
in	O
representative	O
governments	O
like	O
the	O
United	O
States,	O
minority	O
rights	O
are	O
protected:	O
people	O
cannot	O
be	O
deprived	O
of	O
certain	O
rights	O
even	O
if	O
an	O
overwhelming	O
number	O
of	O
people	O
think	O
that	O
they	O
should	O
be.	EOS
For	O
example,	O
let’s	O
say	O
American	O

Why	O
the	O
Division	O
of	O
Labor	O
Increases	O
Production	EOS
When	O
we	O
divide	O
and	O
subdivide	O
the	O
tasks	O
involved	O
with	O
producing	O
a	O
good	O
or	O
service,	O
workers	O
and	O
businesses	O
can	O
produce	O
a	O
greater	O
quantity	O
of	O
output.	EOS

In	O
his	O
observations	O
of	O
pin	O
factories,	O
Smith	O
noticed	O
that	O
one	O
worker	O
alone	O
might	O
make	O
20	O
pins	O
in	O
a	O
day,	O
but	O
that	O

of	O
10	O

(some	O
of	O

to	O

18	O

could	O

48,000	O
pins	O
in	O
a	O
day.	EOS
How	O
can	O

of	O

in	O
certain	O

much	O

than	O
the	O
same	O

who	O

Smith	O

First,	O

in	O
a	O
particular	O
small	O

allows	O

to	O

on	O
the	O

of	O

where	O

an	O

(In	O

by	O

advantage.)	EOS
People	O
have	O
different	O

and	O

so	O
they	O
will	O
be	O
better	O
at	O
some	O
jobs	O
than	O
at	O
others.	EOS

on	O

which	O
are	O
in	O
turn	O
shaped	O
by	O
interests	O
and	O

for	O
